    window.getStringWidth = function(str) {
        var width = len = str.length;
        for(var i=0; i < len; i++) {
            if(str.charCodeAt(i) >= 255) {
                width++;
            }
        }
        return width;
    }

<script src="https://s2.ssl.qhres.com/static/87926952509f4bd1.js"></script><script type="text/javascript">
function _hj_get_cookie(cname) {
  var temp, cookies = document.cookie.split(";");
  for (var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
    temp = cookies[i].split("=");
    if (temp[0].replace(/^\s\s*/, '').replace(/\s\s*$/, '') == cname) {
    	var v = unescape(temp[1]);
    	v = eval('('+v+')');
    	return v;
    }
  }
}
function _hj_set_cookie(cname, cvalue, sec, path, domain, secure) {
  var sec = sec || 1,
  exp = new Date(),
  path = path || "/";
  exp.setTime(exp.getTime() + sec*1000);
  document.cookie = cname + "=" + escape(cvalue) + ";expires= "
  + exp.toGMTString()
  + ((path == null) ? "" : ("; path=" + path))
    + ((domain == null) ? "" : ("; domain=" + domain))
    + ((secure == true) ? "; secure" : "");
}
$(function(){
    var $slide = $('#top-pepper-slide');
    if ($slide.length && parseInt(_hj_get_cookie('_hj_topslds')) != 1) {
        _hj_set_cookie('_hj_topslds', 1, 8*3600);
        $slide.slideDown("slow", function(){
            setTimeout(function(){
                $slide.slideUp("slow");
            }, 3500);
        })
    }
});
</script>
